CROCCHREOT C IH SEKTI L IL SLKEIVLELL L:E VIENLT:E BREMGEINDNIAETRE
GRANNY’S HANKIE TANK | CROCHET SSHHOOPP KKIITT
Straps:
ABBREVIATIONS
Front Right:
Row 1: Join yarn with a sl st in ch-2 sp approx = approximately
of inside corner square #1. Ch 1 (does beg = begin/beginning
not count as st here and throughout).
ch = chain
Work 3 sc in ch-2 sp. Turn. 3 sts.
cont = continue/continuing
Row 2: Ch 1. Work 1 sc in each of next
3 sts. Turn. dc = double crochet
Rep Row 2 until Strap measures 5 (6)" pat = pattern
[12.5 (15) cm]. Fasten off, leaving a tail
rep = repeat
for sewing. Sew Strap to ch-2 sp inside
rnd(s) = round(s)
corner square #3. Weave in ends.
RS = right side
Front Left:
sc = single crochet
Row 1: Join yarn with a sl st in ch-2 sp
of inside corner square #2. Ch 1 (does sl st = slip stitch
not count as st here and throughout). sp(s) = space(s)
Work 3 sc in ch-2 sp. Turn. 3 sts.
st(s) = stitch(es)
Row 2: Ch 1. Work 1 sc in each of next
tog = together
3 sts. Turn.
Rep Row 2 until Strap measures 6 (7)"
[15 (18) cm]. Fasten off, leaving a tail for
sewing. Sew Strap to ch-2 sp inside
corner square #4. Weave in ends.
FINISHING
Neck:
Join yarn to any stitch at back of neck.
Ch 1. Work 1 sc evenly around neckline.
Sl st to first sc to join. Fasten off and
weave in ends.
Armhole:
Join yarn to any stitch at back of
armhole. Ch 1. Work 1 sc evenly around.
Sl st to first sc to join. Fasten off
and weave in ends. Rep for second
armhole.

Designer: Michelle Moore
Michelle Moore is the owner and
designer behind Sentry Box Designs, a
creative haven of fashionable garment
patterns best complemented by luxury
fibres. Michelle launched Sentry Box
Designs in 2017 wanting to offer a way
for makers to take a moment and splurge
on themselves, driving the idea that
crochet can be trendy, fun and modern.
